Bruniquel & Associates Learnership (Boltonia, Krugersdorp)
Qualification:  FETC: Business Administration L4
Start:  1 April 2025
End:  31 March 2026

We are looking for highly committed individuals serious about their future and finding permanent employment.

The skills you acquire during the Learnership will distinguish you from other candidates.

Who will qualify?

* Aged between 18 - 35
* A Grade 12 qualification is essential, with a 50% or higher passing mark for 1st language, 2nd language, and Mathematics/Maths literacy.
* Must not have previously completed the same qualification/learnership at another company or organisation
* Have 1 year of work experience
* South African Citizen
* Employment Equity Candidate
* Must be unemployed
* Present a valid medical record detailing your disability
* Candidates must be willing to commit for 12-month learnership program
* Self-motivated
* Organized
* Results Driven
* Attention to detail
* Good verbal and written communication skills
* Ability to work in a flexible working environment
* Ability to work in a pressurized working environment
* No criminal record or a negative credit record
* Candidates must not be enrolled in any formal full-time studies.
* Must be computer literate 

Ethnic groups include;
- Indian Males and Females  (18 - 35 individuals living with a disability)
- Coloured Males and Females  (18 - 35 individuals living with a disability)
- African Males and Females  (18 - 35 individuals living with a disability)

You will be working and attending classes for 20 days per month in Boltonia, Krugersdorp 

Are you the ideal candidate we are looking for?  

To start your application, please send your CV, ID, Matric Certificate, Medical Note confirming your disability, Proof of SARS number and Proof of Bank Account to rika@pendula.co.za.  Include the reference (April 2025 - BAL4) in the subject line

Please explain why you believe we should select you for a face-to-face interview with your application.

The closing date for applications is 21 March 2025.

Good luck
The Recruitment Team
